yon bdag gi bsnyen bkur dang 'bul ba yang so so nas mang du byung ba rnams kyis dge 'dun kho na skyong zhing gzims spyil du skyid chos mi mdzad /
'on kyang sku mdun du byung ba'i yon bdag thams cad la btsad po la dkar yol dang /
sprang po la pham phabs kyi tshul du rim pa skad de ba gnang /
gdan sa der sa pho stag nas lcags pho stag gi bar lo ngo bcu gsum bzhugs pa la slob ma grub pa'i skyes bu mang du thon /
grwa pa brgyad brgya la gdugs thogs lnga brgya zhes grags /
sngar chos gsung ba'i tshe kho bo'i grwa pa ma 'dus gsung ba dang /
phyis 'bri khung chos rje rten dge bsnyen zhig spyan sngar sleb pa na /
da ni kho'i grwa pa 'dus shes kyang gsung /
chos rje ma byon gong du phyag rgya chen po'i rtogs pa shar ba thams cad mgo la thod pa mi 'gebs bya ba'i bka' stsal yod pa la /
chos rjes phebs nas rtogs ldan skye ba'i 'khor lo bskor ba la sogs pa sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i chos mang du byung bar grags /
de ltar dge 'dun skyong ba'i dus nyid nas gzhan dang gzhan du sku lus kyi bkod pa bcu gnyis su bstan pa dang u rgyan gyi gnas su byon nas mkha'  'gro ma rnams la rgyud sde chen po gsan pa'i rgyud de'i le'u'i grangs dang don bsdu ba'i yi ge yang mdzad /
de la sogs pa phyogs thams cad na kho bo 'dra ba mang por byas nas sems can gyi don byed ces bya ba la sogs pa'i mdzad pa rgya chen po rnams ni gong ma rnams kyi rnam thar na gsal bas 'dir mdo tsam las ma bris so / /
de lta bu'i ston pa gnyis pa de ni lcags pho stag gi zla ba bdun pa'i nyer lnga la sprul pa'i sku bsdu ba mdzad /
de'i tshe ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang /
gdung khri khar gdan drangs pa'i tshe'ang sa chen po g.yos shing /
yon chab rnams phyed phyed tsam po ba dang /
me tog gi char dang /
glu snyan dang /
ngo mtshar ba'i cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung /
sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' mang po lhags pa dang /
dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro 'dus pa'i dag pa'i snang ba'ang grwa pa mang po la shar /
ring bsrel shin du mang po dang /
thugs ljags ma tshig par byon pa la ljags dum bu gnyis su byas nas gdung khang re na bzhugs pa da lta khams na yod gsung /
thugs ni gdung rten bkra shis 'od 'bar na bzhugs pa /
da lta gtsug lag khang gi rten gtso yin /
de la bu chen byon pa ni /
mos gus mthar thug stag lung thang ba /
rtogs pa'i mthar thug sna phu ba /
shes rab mthar thug sbar phu ba /
nus pa'i mthar thug 'chan phu rgya ras rnams la mthar thug gi bu bzhi zer /
skal ldan ye shes seng+ge /
rtogs ldan mi nyag sgom rings /
grub thob nyag re se bo /
kun ldan gtsang pa ras chung  rnams la gdams pa'i bu bzhi zer /
chos rje 'jig rten mgon po /
'ban b+ha phug pa /
chos rje ldum /
chos rje gtum rnams la ro gcig rtogs pa phyed dang bzhi zer /
gshen sgom dkar ba /
myang gshen grong pa /
rngog seng+ge kha ba /
rtsi lung ba rnams la thugs kyi sras bzhi zer /
rin po che shug rtsar ba /
lha sa ba dge 'dun skyabs /
phru ku ston pa blo gros seng+ge /
rgyan thang pa rnams la yi ge ma'i bu bzhi zer /
bla ma dmar ba /
ye phug pa /
dgyer sgom dge ba'i bshes gnyen seng ge dpal rnams la nye ba'i sras bzhi zer /
de dag grangs su bcad de sngon rabs rnams la grags pas brjod pa yin mod kyi /
gzhan yang kun ldan ras pa'i khu bo rin po che rgyal tsha la soT pa dang /
gzhan yang grub rtags du ma ston pa'i dge slong nam mkha' 'od la sogs pa grub pa'i skyes bu mang du byung ba rnams phyogs so so na grags pa che zhing /
phrin las che bar yod kyang /
bla ma gong mas bsdus pa tsam zhig bris pa'o / /
'bri khung sgom pa shAka rin gyis / /
gdan sa dpal gyi phag gru de / /
chu mig brgya rtsa'i mgo bo yin / /
zhes smra ba ltar bod kyi yul 'di'i gtsug lag khang dang sde dgon la sogs pa grangs med pa gdan sa 'di las mched de /
'bri khung chos rje las mched par gyur pa'ang bod khams gsum du bgrang gis ga la lang /
gling ras pa las mched pa 'brug skor rnams kyis kyang bya rgod kyi nyin lam bcu gsum du khyab par grags /
dpal stag lung thang ba las gyes pa'ang dbus dang khams kyi sa char shin du mang por mched /
skal ldan ye shes seng ges bsnubs 'dul ba 'dzin pa rjes su gzung bas g.yam bzangs pa mtha' rgyas dang bcas pa shin tu rgya che /
khams su'ang chos rje dmar bas sho dgon btab pa las tshogs pa nyis stong tsam 'dus shing /
chos rje dmar ba'i rjes su sha yang dgon pa /
rmog spyan snga rin po che /
sha dbu rtse ba /
rnal rin chen gling pa la sogs khyad 'phags mang du byon /
de las brgyud pa'i bu chen yang sgi li chos 'od kyis ri rgya dgon btab /
de'i dgon lag rgyal dgon la sogs mang du yod /
khyad par rnal rin chen gling ba la sbong 'od zer bla mas thug ste thugs thugs rje chen po'i grub thob tu grags /
bum chu'i ril bus bod dang rgya thams cad du khyab /
bu chen rtogs ldan dge ba rgyal mtshan /
dkon mchog rgyal mtshan /
shing mgo ba sogs gzhan don mdzad pa mang du byon no / /
nyag re se bos 'gro mgon dang mjal nas grub pa brnyes te khams su byon nas gles dgon btab /
grub rtags mang du bstan /
'di kar ma pa shi yin zhes kar ma pa shi rang gis zhal gyis bzhes so / /
gshen dgon dkar ba gdung rus gshen /
mtshan rdo rje dbang phyug tsa'i nang na dgon pa btab pas dam shod smad pa zhes grags /
zhang mtshal ba la sogs slob ma mang du byon /
myang gshen grong ba ni /
yar klungs gshen grong ba /
sku na gzhon nu nas rab tu byung /
'gro mgon dang mjal nas gdams pa rdzogs par zhus /
khong rang gi 'khrungs sar sgrub pa mdzad pas mkha' spyod du gshegs /
rngog seng ge kha ba ni /
ljang  seng ge khar dgon pa btab pas seng ge kha par grags /
bla ma'i gdan sa la gnod dogs nas grwa pa rnams bkye nas rang yul du byon /
sku chos nyi zer la 'gel ba soT mdzad pas 'gro don 'phel bar byung /
de'i slob ma dpal chen chos yes yin /
tsi lung bas tsi lung btab ste gzhan don bskyangs /
'jig rten mgon pos rab byung gi slob dpon mdzad /
bla ma rgyan thang pa ni /
'gro mgon dang mjal /
gdams pa mang du gsan /
chos skyong gi sprul pa'i bya rog gis gtor ma khyer sar dgon pa btab nas da lta'i bar du phrin las kyi rgyun ma chad do / /
bla ma ye phug pa ye shes rtsegs ni /
byang rta sna dang lho ye phug shar lho'i rdzong rnams btab /
dgyer sgom gnyis byung ba las gcig gis mal gro phyogs su thugs dam mdzad /
'bri khung chos rjes kyang bsngags pa mang du mdzad pa cig byung ngo / /
bla ma 'brom gyis skam dgos lung btab /
'gro don rgyas par byung ngo / /
'chan bu rgya ras ni /
spyir grub pa brnyes /
khyad par chos skyong gis rjes su gzung ngo / /
mi nyag sgom rings ni /
'gro mgon dang mjal nas khrid gsan gyi yod pa la 'gro mgon gyis kho'i mdun du thag pa'i rgya cig bres /
ral gri cig kyang zhog gsung ba las de dang nye bar spyil bo'i gdong du khong gi pha gsod mi cig yod pa de khong gi rtsar khrid nas 'gro mgon gyis byon pas /
sgom rings zhe sdang skyes te ral gri de khyer nas rgyugs pas /
'gro mgon gyis khyod rang gi zhe sdang gi sems de la ltos gsung ba'i bka' gnang bas de nyid du gnas  lugs kyi rtogs pa khyad par can 'khrungs /
phan sems che bas 'gro mgon gyi slob ma sar ba rnams la'ang sgom lugs legs par slob /
phyis 'bri khung du dgon pa btab nas bzhugs pas grwa pa brgya tsam 'dus /
klog mi mkhyen pas gzhan don la cung zad gnod par byung /
mya ngan las 'da' khar grwa pa rnams kyis ngus pas khyed rnams bla ma ngan du mi 'gro /
g.ye pha gi na pha bong cig gi 'og na dge bsnyen sgom shes pa cig yod /
de bos dang gsung nas gshegs so / /
spar phu ba ni /
g.yo ru grar 'khrungs /
gdung rus rngan /
gzhon nu nas thos bsam mang du mdzad /
khyad par slob dpon phyab la ring du brten pas khong gi slob ma rnams kyi nang nas shes rab che bar grags /
rigs tshogs la bstan bcos mang du brtsams shing bshad pa'ang mdzad /
dus phyis gro shul ba dang mjal /
a su las byung ba'i do has thugs khengs nas yod pa la /
bla ma yel ba ye shes brtsegs kyis do ha'i skor rnams gsan pas /
der yel ba'i thugs la 'di bshad pa rkyang ngu 'dug nga'i bla ma de dang mjal na nyams myong khyad par can yang yong nges bsam nas sbar phu ba la /
'gro mgon gyi spyan sngar thengs gcig 'byon pa 'thad zhus pas /
rang re bas lhag pa cang yod dam gsung pas /
cis kyang 'byon par zhu dang lhag pa'ang 'ong srid zhus pas /
sbar phu ba thugs mnyes pas phag mo grur 'gro mgon gyi drung du mjal /
'gro mgon dang gsung gleng kyang mang du mdzad /
der sbar phu ba'i thugs la /
bla ma 'di sems  tsam gyi lta ba 'dzin par 'dug snyam pa cig byung bas /
'gro mgon gyis mkhyen te /
nga'i chos 'dis nam zhig khyed la phan pa cig 'ong gsung ba'i bka' gnang /
khrid btab pas 'di la nga rang zhib par 'dug snyam nas yon tan ma skyes /
tshogs chos gsan pas de la mgu bar gyur nas log byon pa la /
yang bla ma yel pas /
bla ma rin po che'i drung du mos gus can la yon tan 'char rgyu cig 'ong gi 'dug pa la /
slob dpon pa la ma skyes par snang bas /
da dung lan cig gshegs par zhu byas pas /
de rung gsung nas dpon slob 'grogs nas phag mo grur byon pas /
'gro mgon gyis khong gi thos pas nga rgyal ba de'i 'dzin pa bshig pa'i phyir /
rten 'brel mdzad de /
bu ram la padma'i par legs par btab nas mdzes lam me pa cig mdzad nas drangs /
khong de la chags te ma gsol bar bzhag pas /
der bla ma yel ba bzhengs nas bu ram bcag nas drangs nas /
de gsol bar zhu byas pas de gsol /
de nas 'gro mgon gyi zhal nas /
pha rol tu phyin pa dang dbu ma la sogs pa rnams rgyu mtshan nyid kyi chos /
'bras bu gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa dang thabs lam gyi bye brag dang phyag rgya chen po'i gdams ngag la sogs pa thams cad kyang sems rtogs pa'i thabs su gsungs pa kho na yin /
de rnams kyi don yang sgom dgos pa kho na yin pas bsgoms shig gsung pa la /
ga re gdams ngag ci yang ma bstan pa la bsgoms shig gsung ba ji ltar yin snyam ste /
cung zhig bsams tsa na gnas lugs kyi don mngon du gyur /
'gro mgon la gsol 'debs 'dod 'jo'i ba mo yang mdzad /
phyis sbar phur dgon pa btab /
yi dam gyi lha mang po'ang zhal gzigs /
grub thob tu yang grags /
tshugs pa'ang lnga brgya tsam 'dus /
rang gi rtogs pa dang sangs rgyas kyi rtogs pa gnyis ngo bo la khyad med dgongs nas /
rtogs pa skyed med bya ba'i grub mtha' yang yod /
des na rnal 'byor bzhi po nyams rim yin gyi rtogs pa'i rim pa min zhes gsung /
'di la grub thob gling ras pa la sogs pa'i mched grogs mang pos kyang do ha gsan /
gnyan ras dge 'dun 'bum dang yel ba la sogs mang pos gtugs so / /
yang 'gro mgon gyi slob ma sangs rgyas gnyan ras ni /
'khrungs yul bsam yas khams gsum pa /
gdung rus gnyan yin /
phag mo gru pa dang lo ro ras pa'i slob ma li ras la gdams pa rnams gsan /
ma yul rong gi rdo rang thag gi phug par lo dgu sgrub pa mdzad /
ma yul du mkha' 'gro'i lung bstan bzhin dgon pa btab /
dus phyis lo ro 'phar la du dgon pa btab nas bzhugs /
de'i dpon po rgyal bas kyang ma yul dgon par stan thog gcig du lo dgur sgrub pa mdzad pas dbu skra dang bzhugs gdan gyi bar du srog chags kyi tshang chas ba'ang byung /
ye shes mgon po'i grub pa phul du phyin /
gnyan ras la bla ma rdzong pa sogs sgrub brgyud 'dzin pa mang du byung ngo / /
bla ma zhang ni /
dang por 'gro mgon dang mched grogs yin pa las /
phyis mos pa rnyed nas slob ma mdzad /
se gse ba dang ngang rkyal gyi gtsug lag khang chen po btab /
dge 'dun gyi sde yang bskyangs /
'gro mgon zhi bar gshegs nas gdan sa'i zhabs tog kyang mang du bsgrubs /
'bri khung chos rje'i mkhan po yang mdzad do / /
lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa dang por sa chen las thob nas rang gis yig cha'ang mdzad /
gdams pa de 'dzin pa'i slob rgyud yang rgyun chags su byung 'dug go dpal phag mo gru pa slob ma dang bcas pa'i skabs so / / /
